[30;1m102 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m103 | [0m[35mQuery parameters are actually a type of "multidict", where a given key[0m
[30;1m104 | [0m[35mcan have multiple values. This is why the :meth:`~URL.get()` method[0m
[30;1m105 | [0m[35mreturns a list of strings. Keys can also have no value, which is[0m
[30;1m106 | [0m[35mconventionally interpreted as a truthy flag.[0m
